mukhya rup se iskaa sambandh brihaspati se hota he- sone se urja or garmi donon paidaa hoti he- saath hi sona vish ke prabhaav ko bhi nasht kar detaa he- sona agar laabhadaayak ho to vyakti ko samrudh karata he- parantu agar nuksaan kare to durghatnaayen kara daalata he- keval shauk ke liye sona dhaaran nahin karnaa chahie, aavashyaktaa or laabh ke aadhaar par hi dhaaran karensone ke saath kis tarah kii saavdhaaniyaan rakhni chahie?- jin logon ko pet yaa motaape kii samasya ho, unhen sone ke prayog se bachanaa chahie- krodhi logon ko or jinka jabaan par niyantran na rahata ho aise logon ko bhi sone ke prayog se bachanaa chahie- jinaki kundali main brihaspati karaab ho unako sona dhaaran nahin karnaa chahie- jo log loha,koyala yaa shani sambandhi vyavsaay karte hon , unhen bhi sona dhaaran nahin karnaa chahie- sone kii vastuon kaa daan or uphaar use hi den jo aapkaa priy ho- sone kii bichhiya or paayal dhaaran karne se bachanaa chahie- qamar main sona dhaaran na karen , laal dhaage main sone ke ghunghru bacchon ko pahana sakate hai- swarna ke saath maance or madiraa kaa seven karnaa kadaapi uttam nahin hotenkshay tritiya par sone kii kharidari kaise karen?- sone kii kharidari kaa sabase upyukt samay dopaher kaa hota he- agar sona na kharid saken to sone ke aavaran vaali chizein khariden- saath hi koi na koi dhaatu daan ke liye jarur khariden- pehle kisi nirdhan vyakti ko daan karen- phir swayan kaa sona pehle bhagwaan ko arpit karen- tab jaakar sone kaa prayog karnaa armbh kareshkshay tritiya par sone kaa vishesh prayog?- sone kaa ek chaukor tukdaa banavaaen- is par "shrin" likhvaayen- isko akshay tritiya par maan lakshmi ko arpit karen- maan ke saamne ek vishesh mantra kaa jaap karen- mantra hoga -" hrin shrin kamale kamalaalaye praseed praseed mahalakshmayai namah"- mantra jap ke baad us sone ke tukade ko laal dhaage yaa sone kii chen main gale main dhaaran karen- aapaki sampannataa akshay ho jaayegi
